5 G-RetrieverÂ¶

Figure 3:Overview of the proposed G-Retriever: 1) Indexing: Graphs are indexed for efficient query processing; 2) Retrieval: The most semantically relevant nodes and edges are retrieved, conditioned on the query; 3) Subgraph Construction: A connected subgraph is extracted, covering as many relevant nodes and edges as possible while maintaining a manageable graph size; 4) Generation: An answer is generated using a â€˜graph promptâ€™, a textualized graph, and the query.
